***констатировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:констатировать.html>констати́ровать</a> (7010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">constater</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:констатировать.html>констати́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konstatírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to state</li>
<li>to establish (a fact)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, двувидовой (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образовывать.html>образо́вывать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***конструировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конструировать.html>конструи́ровать</a> (22256)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">konstruieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конструировать.html>конструи́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konstruírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сконструировать.html>сконструи́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to construct, to build, to structure, to design, to form</li></ol>

***конструктивный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конструктивный.html>конструкти́вный</a> (10877)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">конструкти́в</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konstruktív</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cōnstructīvus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cōnstructus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">constructed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конструктивный.html>конструкти́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konstruktívnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>constructive <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">helpful</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конструктивный.html>конструкти́вная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:критика.html>кри́тика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>konstruktívnaja</b> krítika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">constructive criticism</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> construction, constructive</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:консульский.html>ко́нсульский</a> (31493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консул.html>ко́нсул</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kónsul</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консульский.html>ко́нсульский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kónsulʹskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> consul, consulate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in any meaning</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; consular</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:консультация.html>консульта́ция</a> (8231)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консультация.html>консульта́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konsulʹtácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консультация.html>консульта́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консультация.html>консульта́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консультация.html>консульта́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>consultation, advice
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получить.html>получи́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:консультация.html>консульта́цию</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">polučítʹ <b>konsulʹtáciju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get an opinion</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tutorial</li>
<li>consulting room, advisory board, advice bureau, guidance centre
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:юридический.html>юриди́ческая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:консультация.html>консульта́ция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">juridíčeskaja <b>konsulʹtácija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">legal advice office</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тская</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:консультация.html>консульта́ция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">détskaja <b>konsulʹtácija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">children's clinic</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нская</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:консультация.html>консульта́ция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">žénskaja <b>konsulʹtácija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">antenatal clinic, maternity welfare centre</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***контактный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:контактный.html>конта́ктный</a> (19613)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контакт.html>конта́кт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kontákt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контактный.html>конта́ктный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kontáktnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> contact
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:контактный.html>конта́ктные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:линза.html>ли́нзы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kontáktnyje</b> línzy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">contact lenses</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:контактный.html>конта́ктный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:телефон.html>телефо́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kontáktnyj</b> telefón</i> ― <span class="e-translation">contact phone</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>in direct contact
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:контактный.html>конта́ктный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kontáktnyj</b> bolʹnój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">patient in direct contact (with someone)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> easy to establish contact with</li>
<li>helping to establish connections (of a political or commercial nature)</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кон.html>кон</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:такт.html>та́кт</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контингент.html>континге́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kontingént</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контингент.html>континге́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контингент.html>континге́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контингент.html>континге́нтов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>contingent; quota (of troops)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:континентальный.html>континента́льный</a> (29718)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kontinental</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:континентальный.html>континента́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kontinentálʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>continental
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:континентальный.html>континента́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:климат.html>кли́мат</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kontinentálʹnyj</b> klímat</i> ― <span class="e-translation">continental climate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резко.html>ре́зко</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:континентальный.html>континента́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:климат.html>кли́мат</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rézko <b>kontinentálʹnyj</b> klímat</i> ― <span class="e-translation">acutely continental climate</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mainland
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:континентальный.html>континента́льный</a></b> кита́й</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kontinentálʹnyj</b> Kitáj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mainland China</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kontor</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">comptoir</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">compter</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">computāre</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:контра.html>контра</a> (23225)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Clipping of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контрреволюция.html>контрреволю́ция</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kontrrevoljúcija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контра.html>ко́нтра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kóntra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контра.html>ко́нтры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контра.html>ко́нтры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контра.html>ко́нтр</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> often collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> counterrevolutionary, counterrevolutionaries; counterrevolution (especially in reference to 1917 <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_Revolution" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Russian Revolution">Russian Revolution</a>).</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Clipping of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контрольный.html>контро́льная</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kontrólʹnaja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контра.html>контра́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kontrá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контра.html>контры́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контра.html>контры́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контра.html>ко́нтр</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (a small) school test
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контрольный.html>контро́льная</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kontrólʹnaja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контрольный.html>контро́льная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kontrólʹnaja rabóta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кон.html>кон</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тра́</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1b  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-контр-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:контрабандный.html>контраба́ндный</a> (21814)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контрабандный.html>контраба́ндный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kontrabándnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>contraband
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:контрабандный.html>контраба́ндный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kontrabándnyj</b> továr</i> ― <span class="e-translation">contraband; contraband/smuggled goods</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***контракт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:контракт.html>контра́кт</a> (4518)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kontrakt</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kontrakt</i>, from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">contractus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контракт.html>контра́кт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kontrákt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контракт.html>контра́кта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контракт.html>контра́кты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:контракт.html>контра́ктов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">контра́ктный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>contract, agreement</li></ol>
